comprehensive query result caching layer in the `pkg/services/caching` package that provides an abstraction over multiple cache backends. Here's a detailed breakdown of the architecture:\\n\\n### 1. Cache Service Interface and Abstraction\\nThe core caching interface is defined in `pkg/services/caching/service.go` with the `CachingService` interface that supports:\\n- `HandleQueryRequest()` - Checks cache for existing query results and returns an update function if cache miss\\n- `HandleResourceRequest()` - Similar caching for resource requests\\n\\nThe OSS implementation (`OSSCachingService`) provides a no-op implementation, while the `CachingServiceClient` wraps this with request handling and metrics collection.\\n\\n### 2. Cache Key Generation\\nCache keys are generated in `pkg/services/caching/service.go::GetKey()` using:\\n- **Namespace and prefix support**: Keys are formatted as `namespace:prefix:hash`\\n- **JSON Encoding**: The `JSONEncoder` struct encodes query objects to JSON using `json.NewEncoder()`\\n- **SHA256 Hashing**: The `SHA256KeyFunc()` function creates a SHA256 hash of the encoded JSON, producing a consistent, collision-resistant key\\n- The encoded key format ensures deterministic cache key generation for identical queries\\n\\n### 3. Cache Backend Abstraction (Redis, Memcached, In-Memory)\\nThe remote cache abstraction is implemented in `pkg/infra/remotecache/` with:\\n\\n**RemoteCache Interface** (`remotecache.go`):\\n- `CacheStorage` interface defines Get/Set/Delete operations for byte arrays\\n- Supports configurable backends via `RemoteCacheSettings` configuration\\n\\n**Backend Implementations**:\\n- **Redis** (`redis_storage.go`): Redis client-based distributed caching\\n- **Memcached** (`memcached_storage.go`): Memcached protocol support\\n- **Database** (`database_storage.go`): SQL database-backed caching for single-instance deployments\\n- **Local In-Memory** (`pkg/infra/localcache/cache.go`): Go-cache based local caching with configurable TTL and cleanup intervals\\n\\n**Decorator Pattern**:\\n- `prefixCacheStorage`: Adds a prefix to all cache keys\\n- `encryptedCacheStorage`: Wraps cache values with encryption/decryption using the secrets service\\n\\n### 4. Cache TTL Policy\\nTTL (Time-To-Live) policies are implemented through:\\n- **Default TTL**: 24 hours (`defaultMaxCacheExpiration`) in `remotecache.go` when not specified\\n- **Query-Specific TTL**: Set via `time.Duration` parameter in `cache.Set()` calls\\n- **Configuration**: Defined in `pkg/setting/setting.go` and `pkg/plugins/models.go::QueryCachingConfig`\\n- **QueryCachingConfig struct**: Contains `Enabled` boolean and `TTLMS` (milliseconds) for datasource-specific caching\\n- **Panel-Level Override**: The `queryCachingTTL` field in dashboard panel queries allows per-query TTL overrides\\n\\n### 5. Cache Invalidation on Dashboard Save\\nCache invalidation follows these patterns:\\n- **Delete Operations**: Cache items are removed via `CacheStorage.Delete(ctx context.Context, key string) error`\\n- **Metrics Tracking**: `pkg/services/caching/metrics.go` tracks cache operations with Prometheus histograms:\\n  - `query_caching_request_duration_seconds` - Query cache performance\\n  - `resource_caching_request_duration_seconds` - Resource cache performance\\n- **Cache Status Headers**: X-Cache header set to HIT/MISS/BYPASS/ERROR/DISABLED values\\n- **Event-Based Invalidation**: Dashboard save events trigger cache invalidation through event bus listeners (Enterprise feature)\\n\\n### 6. Request Flow and Integration\\n**Query Execution Path** (`service.go::WithQueryDataCaching`):\\n1. CachingServiceClient receives a QueryDataRequest\\n2. Calls `HandleQueryRequest()` to check cache\\n3. If cache hit: returns cached response\\n4. If cache miss: executes query via provided function\\n5. Updates cache with result via `UpdateCacheFn` callback\\n6. Sets X-Cache response header with status\\n7. Records metrics for performance monitoring\\n\\n**Response Caching**:\\n- Type: `CachedQueryDataResponse` contains the cached response and an `UpdateCacheFn` callback\\n- Conditional Caching: Uses feature flag `FlagAwsAsyncQueryCaching` to determine when to cache async query results\\n- Error Handling: Only caches successful responses (nil error)\\n\\n### 7. Configuration and Settings\\nCache configuration is managed in:\\n- `pkg/setting/setting.go`: RemoteCacheSettings for backend selection\\n- `conf/defaults.ini` and `conf/sample.ini`: Configuration file templates\\n- Supported backends: `redis`, `memcached`, `database`, `memory`\\n- Encryption support: Optional cache value encryption via secrets service\\n- Prefix support: Configurable key prefix for namespace isolation\\n\\n### 8. Testing Support\\n- `pkg/services/caching/fake_caching_service.go`: Mock implementation for testing\\n- `pkg/services/caching/service_test.go`: Unit tests covering caching behavior\\n- Remote cache backends have dedicated test files (`*_test.go` and `*_integration_test.go`)\\n\\nThe architecture enables Grafana to efficiently cache query results across multiple datasources while supporting both single-instance deployments (local cache) and distributed deployments (Redis/Memcached), with enterprise features handling cache invalidation tied to dashboard lifecycle events.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":1821,"cache_read_input_tokens":115332,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":1821},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"c165451c-0a77-48df-b0a0-b57d4d1d4337","uuid":"8f05a669-0aa3-4fc8-acdb-c51185e53eb9"}

Cache Backend Abstraction (Redis, Memcached, In-Memory)\\nThe remote cache abstraction is implemented in `pkg/infra/remotecache/` with:\\n\\n**RemoteCache Interface** (`remotecache.go`):\\n- `CacheStorage` interface defines Get/Set/Delete operations for byte arrays\\n- Supports configurable backends via `RemoteCacheSettings` configuration\\n\\n**Backend Implementations**:\\n- **Redis** (`redis_storage.go`): Redis client-based distributed caching\\n- **Memcached** (`memcached_storage.go`): Memcached protocol support\\n- **Database** (`database_storage.go`): SQL database-backed caching for single-instance deployments\\n- **Local In-Memory** (`pkg/infra/localcache/cache.go`): Go-cache based local caching with configurable TTL and cleanup intervals\\n\\n**Decorator Pattern**:\\n- `prefixCacheStorage`: Adds a prefix to all cache keys\\n- `encryptedCacheStorage`: Wraps cache values with encryption/decryption using the secrets service\\n\\n### 4. Cache TTL Policy\\nTTL (Time-To-Live) policies are implemented through:\\n- **Default TTL**: 24 hours (`defaultMaxCacheExpiration`) in `remotecache.go` when not specified\\n- **Query-Specific TTL**: Set via `time.Duration` parameter in `cache.Set()` calls\\n- **Configuration**: Defined in `pkg/setting/setting.go` and `pkg/plugins/models.go::QueryCachingConfig`\\n- **QueryCachingConfig struct**: Contains `Enabled` boolean and `TTLMS` (milliseconds) for datasource-specific caching\\n- **Panel-Level Override**: The `queryCachingTTL` field in dashboard panel queries allows per-query TTL overrides\\n\\n### 5. Cache Invalidation on Dashboard Save\\nCache invalidation follows these patterns:\\n- **Delete Operations**: Cache items are removed via `CacheStorage.Delete(ctx context.Context, key string) error`\\n- **Metrics Tracking**: `pkg/services/caching/metrics.go` tracks cache operations with Prometheus histograms:\\n  - `query_caching_request_duration_seconds` - Query cache performance\\n  - `resource_caching_request_duration_seconds` - Resource cache performance\\n- **Cache Status Headers**: X-Cache header set to HIT/MISS/BYPASS/ERROR/DISABLED values\\n- **Event-Based Invalidation**: Dashboard save events trigger cache invalidation through event bus listeners (Enterprise feature)\\n\\n### 6. Request Flow and Integration\\n**Query Execution Path** (`service.go::WithQueryDataCaching`):\\n1. CachingServiceClient receives a QueryDataRequest\\n2. Calls `HandleQueryRequest()` to check cache\\n3. If cache hit: returns cached response\\n4. If cache miss: executes query via provided function\\n5. Updates cache with result via `UpdateCacheFn` callback\\n6. Sets X-Cache response header with status\\n7. Records metrics for performance monitoring\\n\\n**Response Caching**:\\n- Type: `CachedQueryDataResponse` contains the cached response and an `UpdateCacheFn` callback\\n- Conditional Caching: Uses feature flag `FlagAwsAsyncQueryCaching` to determine when to cache async query results\\n- Error Handling: Only caches successful responses (nil error)\\n\\n### 7. Configuration and Settings\\nCache configuration is managed in:\\n- `pkg/setting/setting.go`: RemoteCacheSettings for backend selection\\n- `conf/defaults.ini` and `conf/sample.ini`: Configuration file templates\\n- Supported backends: `redis`, `memcached`, `database`, `memory`\\n- Encryption support: Optional cache value encryption via secrets service\\n- Prefix support: Configurable key prefix for namespace isolation\\n\\n### 8. Testing Support\\n- `pkg/services/caching/fake_caching_service.go`: Mock implementation for testing\\n- `pkg/services/caching/service_test.go`: Unit tests covering caching behavior\\n- Remote cache backends have dedicated test files (`*_test.go` and `*_integration_test.go`)\\n\\nThe architecture enables Grafana to efficiently cache query results across multiple datasources while supporting both single-instance deployments (local cache) and distributed deployments (Redis/Memcached), with enterprise features handling cache invalidation tied to dashboard lifecycle events.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}
